## <a name="windows-server-2003-r2"></a><span data-ttu-id="57aea-706">Windows Server 2003 R2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57aea-706">Windows Server 2003 R2</span></span>

-   [<span data-ttu-id="57aea-707">Атрибуты</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57aea-707">Attributes</span></span>](#windows-server-2003-r2-attributes)

## <a name="windows-server-2008-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="57aea-1063">Атрибуты Windows Server 2008</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57aea-1063">Windows Server 2008 Attributes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57aea-1064">Этот класс содержит следующие атрибуты для Windows Server 2008:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57aea-1064">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2008:</span></span>
